\"\"\"\n   598→    pb = item.get(\"pendingBattle\") or {}\n   599→    atk = find_card(item, pb.get(\"attackerId\"))\n   600→    tgt_id = pb.get(\"blockerId\") or pb.get(\"targetId\")\n   601→    tgt =       })\n   616→\n   617→    # ----- ② ユニット vs ユニット の場合 -----\n   618→    else:\n   619→        atk_pow = calc_total_power(atk)\n   620→        tgt_pow = calc_total_power(tgt)\n   621→\n   622→ \"payload\": {\"playerId\": tgt[\"ownerId\"], \"amount\": overflow},\n   630→                    })\n   631→        elif atk_pow < tgt_pow:  # 負け\n   632→            destroy_ids.append(atk[\"id\"])\n =============================\n   684→def lambda_handler(event, context):\n   685→    field=event[\"info\"][\"fieldName\"]; args=event.get(\"arguments\",{})\n   686→    logger.info(\"Field %s  Args   \n   720→    # pendingDeferred の初期化\n   721→    item.setdefault(\"pendingDeferred\", [])\n   722→\n   723→    # -------- getMatch ----------------------------------------\n   724→    if field ==
